# I-cd-567 — STRUCTURAL GATE FIX (Codex consult verdict 2026-05-20)

## Verdict: Option D (operator-held admin) + auto-merge-on-green

### INTERIM RULE (effective immediately, until Option D is live)
**Claude STOPS auto-merging. Queue every PR for operator merge.** The
SHA-pinned codex_diff discipline is review EVIDENCE, not merge permission.
The #709 incident proves soft enforcement is not the control boundary.

### Claude can do (engineering, queued for operator merge)
- PR mirroring codex-required.yml + codex_artifact_gate.yml onto `main` (default branch) so Actions registers them.
- Stable unique job/check names.
- CODEOWNERS / ruleset files via PR.

### Operator MUST do (admin — Claude cannot + must not)
- Remove Admin/Maintain/bypass from sotaleung-wec + aldrinor (drop to Write/Triage).
- Apply polaris branch protection: required checks bound to the GitHub Actions App app_id (not bare contexts — Claude must not be able to set commit statuses), enforce/no-bypass ON, required PR review, required conversation resolution.
- Hold the ONLY admin token; revoke/replace Claude tokens with non-admin, non-workflow-write.
- Enable auto-merge (so green codex-required auto-merges without Claude bypassing).

### Why
enforce_admins=false + Claude holding the aldrinor admin token = the
agent-as-execution-engine + agent-as-certification-oracle anti-pattern
(the 28-commits failure). Codex review is currently honored only because
Claude chooses to. Not structural until Claude cannot bypass OR alter
branch protection.

---

## MERGE-AUTHORITY PROTOCOL (Codex decision 2026-05-20, operator-directed)

**DECISION: "Codex decides → Claude executes → operator owns" is ACCEPTED as an INTERIM bridge.** Permanent design is still Option D (operator admin lockdown). It breaks the dangerous coupling (Claude no longer certifies its OWN merge — Codex does) but is not a hard boundary while Claude holds an admin-capable token.

### Claude may merge a PR ONLY when ALL hold:
1. **Codex explicitly authorized** — final decision says `MERGE AUTHORIZED`; BOTH brief + diff tracks APPROVE; approval is for the exact committed head SHA + base.
2. **Canonical diff integrity** — codex_diff.patch exists; its canonical-diff-sha256 matches the actual PR diff; head SHA unchanged since approval. Any mismatch/regenerate/force-push VOIDS approval.
3. **Required CI green** — codex-required SUCCESSFUL, not merely present. Failing/skipped/cancelled/pending/missing/stale BLOCKS. No admin bypass around red/absent checks.
4. **No unresolved blockers** — no Codex REJECT/BLOCK/must-fix; no conflicts; no signing/provenance failure; no unreviewed commits after approval.
5. **Claude posts the decision verbatim in the PR before merging** — PR#, head SHA, base, canonical diff SHA, CI state, exact Codex decision text.
6. **Ordinary auditable merge** — normal merge method; no force-push/history-rewrite/branch-swap/manual-patch; if mechanics need admin bypass → BLOCKED, operator-only.

### OPERATOR-ONLY exclusion list (Claude may NEVER merge, even on Codex APPROVE):
- branch protection / rulesets / permissions / deploy keys / app+token config
- `.github/workflows/**` / CI policy / required-check defs / merge automation
- `CODEOWNERS` / ownership / approval routing
- `polaris-controls/**` / governance / control-plane
- auth / authz / signing keys / secrets / tokens / credentials
- release signing / provenance / attestation / publishing / deploy authority
- anything granting Claude/automation/CI broader write/admin
- emergency/security changes where bypass pressure is part of the ask
- any Claude-authored PR modifying the rules governing Claude's own authority

### #709 would have been BLOCKED under this protocol
(codex-required was RED + SHA mismatch + no verbatim decision posted). The protocol's preconditions 2+3+5 each independently catch it.

  26: # so FastAPI Depends() identity matches what app.dependency_overrides keys on.
  27: # A lambda Depends would be a DIFFERENT callable than get_sign_fn — the
  28: # create_app() override wouldn't fire and the endpoint would always 503.
  29: from polaris_graph.api.audit_bundle_route import (
  30:     build_audit_bundle_response,
  31:     get_sign_fn,
  32: )
  33: from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_slice_chain import (
  34:     SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError,
  35:     build_slice_chain,
  36: )
  37: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  38: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import EvidenceContract
  39: 
  40: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["bundle"])
  41: 
  42: _FIXTURE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[3] / "tests" / "v6" / "fixtures" / "evidence_contract_v1"
  43: 
  44: _GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX = {
  45:     "golden_clinical_001": "golden_run_clinical.json",
  46:     "golden_housing_002": "golden_run_with_contradiction.json",
  47:     "golden_abort_003": "golden_run_abort_no_verified.json",
  48:     "golden_defense_004": "golden_run_defense.json",
  49:     "golden_climate_005": "golden_run_climate.json",
  50:     "golden_ai_006": "golden_run_ai_sovereignty.json",
  51:     "golden_with_drop_reason": "golden_run_with_drop_reason.json",
  52: }
  53: 
  54: 
  55: def load_evidence_contract_for_run(run_id: str) -> EvidenceContract:
  56:     """Resolve a run_id → EvidenceContract for golden fixtures AND real runs.
  57: 
  58:     I-cd-680 (Codex Option B): golden fixtures load from JSON; real completed
  59:     runs resolve run_id → artifact_dir via run_store and build the contract
  60:     from the slice-chain (the same proven path as bundle.tar.gz). Shared by
  61:     the bundle, follow-up (#542), and compare (#543) endpoints so all three
  62:     work on real runs, not just fixtures.
  63: 
  64:     Raises HTTPException(404) for unknown / not-completed / artifact-missing
  65:     runs, HTTPException(422) when the sovereignty cascade empties the report.
  66:     """
  67:     fixture_name = _GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX.get(run_id)
  68:     if fixture_name is not None:
  69:         raw = json.loads((_FIXTURE_DIR / fixture_name).read_text())
  70:         return EvidenceContract.model_validate(raw)
  71: 
  72:     run = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  73:     if run is None:
  74:         raise HTTPException(
  75:             status_code=404,
  76:             detail=(
  77:                 f"Run {run_id!r} not found. Available golden fixtures: "
  78:                 f"{list(_GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX)}."
  79:             ),
  80:         )
  81:     if run.lifecycle_status != "completed" or not run.artifact_dir:
  82:         raise HTTPException(
  83:             status_code=404,
  84:             detail=(
  85:                 f"Run {run_id!r} is not a completed run with artifacts "
  86:                 f"(lifecycle_status={run.lifecycle_status!r})."
  87:             ),
  88:         )
  89: 
  90:     # Import here to avoid a heavy import at module load (build_slice_chain
  91:     # pulls in the audit_ir + clinical generator/retrieval stack).
  92:     from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_evidence_contract import (
  93:         build_evidence_contract_from_artifact,
  94:     )
  95: 
  96:     try:
  97:         return build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
  98:             Path(run.artifact_dir),
  99:             run_id=run.run_id,
 100:             template=run.template or "custom",
 101:             question=run.question or "",
 102:             queued_at=str(run.queued_at or ""),
 103:             finished_at=str(run.finished_at or ""),
 104:             pipeline_status=run.pipeline_status or "success",
 105:         )
 106:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 107:         raise HTTPException(
 108:             status_code=422,
 109:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} has no shippable sections after the "
 110:             f"sovereignty cascade: {exc}",
 111:         ) from exc
 112:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 113:         raise HTTPException(
 114:             status_code=404,
 115:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} artifact_dir is missing required files: {exc}",
 116:         ) from exc
 117: 
 118: 
 119: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle", response_model=EvidenceContract)
 120: def get_bundle(run_id: str) -> EvidenceContract:
 121:     # I-cd-680: real runs now resolve to a typed EvidenceContract built from
 122:     # the slice-chain (was 404-with-pointer-to-bundle.tar.gz). Golden
 123:     # fixtures unchanged.
 124:     return load_evidence_contract_for_run(run_id)

 126: 
 127: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz")
 128: def get_run_bundle_targz(
 129:     run_id: str,
 130:     sign_fn=Depends(get_sign_fn),
 131: ):
 132:     """Resolve run_id → artifact_dir → signed audit bundle (tar.gz).
 133: 
 134:     I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-1 P1-001: `Depends(get_sign_fn)` MUST use
 135:     the actual `get_sign_fn` callable from audit_bundle_route — the
 136:     create_app() registers `app.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn]` to
 137:     inject the real GPGSigner when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set. A lambda
 138:     Depends would be a different callable; the override would never fire.
 139: 
 140:     Status codes:
 141:         200: bundleable run; returns application/gzip
 142:         404: run not found, not completed, or artifact_dir missing
 143:         422: run aborted (pipeline_status=abort_*) or sovereignty cascade
 144:              emptied the report
 145:         503: GPG signer not configured (POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID unset) — surfaced
 146:              by the inner build_audit_bundle_response when sign_fn is None.
 147:     """
 148:     info = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 149:     if info is None:
 150:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail={"error": "run not found"})
 151:     if info.lifecycle_status != "completed":
 152:         raise HTTPException(
 153:             status_code=404,
 154:             detail={"error": f"run not completed: lifecycle_status={info.lifecycle_status}"},
 155:         )
 156:     if info.pipeline_status and info.pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
 157:         raise HTTPException(
 158:             status_code=422,
 159:             detail={"error": f"run aborted: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status}", "bundleable": False},
 160:         )
 161:     if not info.artifact_dir:
 162:         raise HTTPException(
 163:             status_code=404, detail={"error": "run has no artifact_dir recorded"}
 164:         )
 165: 
 166:     artifact_dir = Path(info.artifact_dir)
 167:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
 168:         raise HTTPException(
 169:             status_code=404,
 170:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}"},
 171:         )
 172: 
 173:     # I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-2 P1-002 fix: release_allowed gate.
 174:     # The slice-chain pipeline_verdict collapses partial_* into "success",
 175:     # but a release-blocked partial (e.g. partial_evaluator_advisory with
 176:     # release_allowed=false) MUST NOT ship as a clean bundle. Read the raw
 177:     # manifest.release_allowed flag and refuse with 422 when False.
 178:     try:
 179:         manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 180:     except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError) as exc:
 181:         raise HTTPException(
 182:             status_code=404,
 183:             detail={"error": f"manifest.json missing or invalid: {exc}"},
 184:         ) from exc
 185:     if not manifest_raw.get("release_allowed", False):
 186:         raise HTTPException(
 187:             status_code=422,
 188:             detail={
 189:                 "error": (
 190:                     f"run release-blocked: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status!r}, "
 191:                     f"release_allowed=False. Bundle cannot ship until release gate clears."
 192:                 ),
 193:                 "bundleable": False,
 194:                 "pipeline_status": info.pipeline_status,
 195:             },
 196:         )
 197: 
 198:     try:
 199:         decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
 200:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 201:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail={"error": str(exc)}) from exc
 202:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 203:         raise HTTPException(
 204:             status_code=404,
 205:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir incomplete: {exc}"},
 206:         ) from exc
 207: 
 208:     # I-gen-004 (#496): include the run's reasoning trace in the signed
 209:     # bundle when present. Write-through means the file exists for every
 210:     # completed run; it is hashed under content_type=reasoning_trace.
 211:     extra_files: dict[str, tuple[bytes, str]] | None = None
 212:     trace_path = artifact_dir / "reasoning_trace.jsonl"
 213:     if trace_path.is_file():
 214:         extra_files = {
 215:             "reasoning_trace.jsonl": (
 216:                 trace_path.read_bytes(),
 217:                 "reasoning_trace",
 218:             )
 219:         }
 220: 
 221:     return build_audit_bundle_response(
 222:         decision, pool, report, sign_fn, extra_files=extra_files,
 223:     )

 succeeded in 1766ms:
   1: """I-cd-680 — bridge a real pipeline-A artifact_dir to a typed EvidenceContract.
   2: 
   3: Reuses `build_slice_chain` (I-arch-001d, the same path `GET /runs/{id}/
   4: bundle.tar.gz` already proves on real runs) and maps the slice-chain into the
   5: `EvidenceContract` v1.0 schema that the follow-up (#542) and compare (#543)
   6: endpoints consume.
   7: 
   8: Scope (Codex Option B, 2026-05-20): real-run RESOLUTION only. We do NOT
   9: synthesize rich source-document char offsets — pipeline-A does not record
  10: them. `SourceSpan.span_start`/`span_end` are the truthful 0..len(span_text)
  11: offsets of the recorded evidence text within ITSELF (the recorded quote IS
  12: the span). Rich offsets into the original source body are the deferred
  13: Phase-2 capability (#710), NOT fabricated here (LAW II).
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import json
  19: from pathlib import Path
  20: from typing import Any
  21: 
  22: from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_slice_chain import build_slice_chain
  23: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import (
  24:     ContradictionRecord,
  25:     EvidenceContract,
  26:     SourceSpan,
  27:     VerifiedSentence,
  28: )
  29: 
  30: 
  31: def _read_contradictions(artifact_dir: Path) -> list[ContradictionRecord]:
  32:     """Load contradictions.json if present. Real pipeline-A runs write a list
  33:     of contradiction records; absent/empty → no contradictions."""
  34:     path = artifact_dir / "contradictions.json"
  35:     if not path.exists():
  36:         return []
  37:     try:
  38:         raw = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  39:     except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):
  40:         return []
  41:     records: list[ContradictionRecord] = []
  42:     items = raw if isinstance(raw, list) else raw.get("contradictions", [])
  43:     for i, item in enumerate(items if isinstance(items, list) else []):
  44:         if not isinstance(item, dict):
  45:             continue
  46:         try:
  47:             records.append(
  48:                 ContradictionRecord(
  49:                     contradiction_id=str(item.get("contradiction_id") or f"c{i}"),
  50:                     section_id=str(item.get("section_id") or "unknown"),
  51:                     claim_a=str(item.get("claim_a") or ""),
  52:                     claim_b=str(item.get("claim_b") or ""),
  53:                     evidence_a=[str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_a") or [])],
  54:                     evidence_b=[str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_b") or [])],
  55:                     resolution=item.get("resolution")
  56:                     if item.get("resolution")
  57:                     in ("unresolved", "claim_a_preferred", "claim_b_preferred", "noted_both")
  58:                     else "noted_both",
  59:                 )
  60:             )
  61:         except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a malformed record is skipped, not fatal
  62:             continue
  63:     return records
  64: 
  65: 
  66: def build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
  67:     artifact_dir: Path,
  68:     *,
  69:     run_id: str,
  70:     template: str,
  71:     question: str,
  72:     queued_at: str,
  73:     finished_at: str,
  74:     pipeline_status: str,
  75: ) -> EvidenceContract:
  76:     """Synthesize a fully-valid EvidenceContract from a REAL artifact_dir.
  77: 
  78:     Run metadata (run_id/template/question/timestamps/status) is supplied by
  79:     the caller from run_store (the authoritative source); the evidence + the
  80:     verified sentences come from the slice-chain.
  81: 
  82:     Raises FileNotFoundError / SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError from
  83:     build_slice_chain — the caller maps these to 404 / 422.
  84:     """
  85:     _decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
  86: 
  87:     evidence_pool: list[SourceSpan] = []
  88:     for src in pool.sources:
  89:         # The recorded evidence text. build_slice_chain only admits T1
  90:         # legal-cleared sources, so source_tier is within SourceSpan's
  91:         # T1/T2/T3 Literal.
  92:         span_text = src.full_text or src.snippet or src.title or "n/a"
  93:         evidence_pool.append(
  94:             SourceSpan(
  95:                 evidence_id=src.source_id,
  96:                 source_url=str(src.url),
  97:                 source_tier=src.tier.value,
  98:                 # Truthful self-offset of the recorded span; rich
  99:                 # source-document offsets are deferred to #710.
 100:                 span_start=0,
 101:                 span_end=len(span_text),
 102:                 span_text=span_text,
 103:             )
 104:         )
 105: 
 106:     verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
 107:     for section in report.sections:
 108:         for sent in section.verified_sentences:
 109:             verified_sentences.append(
 110:                 VerifiedSentence(
 111:                     section_id=sent.section_id,
 112:                     sentence_text=sent.sentence_text,
 113:                     provenance_tokens=list(sent.provenance_tokens),
 114:                     # The slice-chain records a single verifier_pass (Local AND
 115:                     # Global must both hold for a sentence to pass strict_verify),
 116:                     # so it maps to both EvidenceContract flags.
 117:                     verifier_local_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
 118:                     verifier_global_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
 119:                     drop_reason=sent.drop_reason,
 120:                 )
 121:             )
 122: 
 123:     return EvidenceContract(
 124:         run_id=run_id,
 125:         template=template,
 126:         question=question,
 127:         queued_at=queued_at,
 128:         finished_at=finished_at,
 129:         pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
 130:         evidence_pool=evidence_pool,
 131:         verified_sentences=verified_sentences,
 132:         frame_coverage=[],
 133:         contradictions=_read_contradictions(artifact_dir),
 134:         cost_usd=float(report.cost_usd or 0.0),
 135:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
 136:         verifier_model=report.evaluator_model,
 137:         family_segregation_passed=report.family_segregation_passed,
 138:     )

  23:     right = load_evidence_contract_for_run(right_run_id)
  24:     return asdict(compare_reports(left, right))

   2: Pydantic models (ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, VerifiedReport) consumable by
   3: the audit-bundle POST endpoint.
   4: 
   5: The audit-bundle path expects the slice-001/002/003 Pydantic shapes, but
   6: pipeline-A produces a different artifact set (manifest.json + report.md +
   7: bibliography.json + contradictions.json + verification_details.json +
   8: evidence_pool.json). This module translates one to the other.
   9: 
  10: Sovereignty cascade (Codex iter-2 P1-001): non-cleared sources are excluded
  11: from pool.sources entirely. Sentences whose provenance_tokens cite an
  12: excluded source are marked verifier_pass=False + drop_reason="invalid_token"
  13: + evaluator_agrees=False. Sections with no remaining passing sentences are
  14: marked section_status="dropped". If ALL sections drop, raises
  15: SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError so the endpoint can return 422.
  16: """

  57:     from polaris_graph.clinical_generator.provenance import (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
  58:         PROVENANCE_TOKEN_RE as _CANONICAL_TOKEN_RE,

  62:     # NOTE: align with polaris_graph.clinical_generator.provenance shape:

  64:     _PROV_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\[#ev:([^:\]]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]")
  65: 
  66: 
  67: class SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError(RuntimeError):
  68:     """Raised when sovereignty cascade leaves no non-dropped sections.
  69: 
  70:     The endpoint catches this and returns 422 to the client. The
  71:     bundle would otherwise fail `assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared`
  72:     or generate an empty pipeline_verdict='success' report — both
  73:     audit-grade incorrect.
  74:     """
  75: 
  76: 
  77: # I-arch-001d Codex iter-4 P2: expanded drop_reason map covering pipeline-A's
  78: # observed reasons including no_integer_overlap / no_content_word_overlap /
  79: # trial_name_mismatch.
  80: _DROP_REASON_MAP: dict[str, DropReason] = {
  81:     "invalid_token": "invalid_token",
  82:     "span_out_of_range": "span_out_of_range",
  83:     "numeric_mismatch": "numeric_mismatch",
  84:     "number_not_in_any_cited_span": "numeric_mismatch",
  85:     "no_integer_overlap_any_cited_span": "numeric_mismatch",
  86:     "overlap_too_low": "overlap_too_low",
  87:     "low_content_overlap": "overlap_too_low",
  88:     "no_content_word_overlap_any_cited_span": "overlap_too_low",
  89:     "no_provenance_token": "no_provenance_token",
  90:     "missing_provenance": "no_provenance_token",
  91:     "entailment_failed": "entailment_failed",
  92:     "trial_name_mismatch": "invalid_token",
  93: }
  94: 
  95: 
  96: def _normalize_drop_reason(raw: str | None) -> DropReason | None:
  97:     if raw is None:
  98:         return None
  99:     base = raw.split(":")[0].strip().lower()
 100:     return _DROP_REASON_MAP.get(base, "invalid_token")
 101: 
 102: 
 103: def _normalize_tier(raw: str) -> tuple[SourceTier, str]:
 104:     """Map pipeline-A tier to SourceTier Literal. T4+/UNKNOWN → T3."""
 105:     upper = (raw or "").upper().strip()
 106:     if upper in ("T1", "T2", "T3"):
 107:         return SourceTier(upper), upper
 108:     return SourceTier.T3, upper or "UNKNOWN"
 109: 
 110: 
 111: def _derive_scope_class(domain: str | None, scope_class: str | None) -> ScopeClassValue:
 112:     """Derive a valid ScopeClassValue Literal from pipeline-A manifest fields."""
 113:     if scope_class:
 114:         s = scope_class.strip().lower()
 115:         for valid in (
 116:             "clinical_efficacy", "clinical_safety", "clinical_diagnosis",
 117:             "clinical_prognosis", "out_of_scope", "uncertain",
 118:         ):
 119:             if s == valid:
 120:                 return valid  # type: ignore[return-value]
 121:     if domain and "clinical" in domain.lower():
 122:         return "clinical_efficacy"
 123:     return "uncertain"
 124: 
 125: 
 126: def _redact_sentence(sent: VerifiedSentence) -> VerifiedSentence:
 127:     """Mark a sentence as failed during sovereignty cascade.
 128: 
 129:     Rebuilds via constructor (runs validators) instead of model_copy
 130:     which bypasses them. Sets evaluator_agrees=False to satisfy the
 131:     invariant that verifier_pass=False forbids evaluator_agrees=True.
 132:     """
 133:     fields = sent.model_dump()
 134:     fields["verifier_pass"] = False
 135:     fields["drop_reason"] = "invalid_token"
 136:     fields["evaluator_agrees"] = False
 137:     return VerifiedSentence(**fields)
 138: 
 139: 
 140: def _evidence_ids_in_tokens(provenance_tokens: list[str]) -> set[str]:
 141:     out: set[str] = set()
 142:     for tok in provenance_tokens:
 143:         m = _PROV_TOKEN_RE.search(tok)
 144:         if m:
 145:             out.add(m.group(1))
 146:     return out
 147: 
 148: 
 149: def _tokens_to_strings(tokens: tuple[EvidenceSpanToken, ...]) -> list[str]:
 150:     return [f"[#ev:{t.evidence_id}:{t.start}-{t.end}]" for t in tokens]
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def _read_optional_json(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None:
 154:     if not path.is_file():
 155:         return None
 156:     try:
 157:         return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 158:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
 159:         return None
 160: 
 161: 
 162: def _full_text_for_evidence_id(
 163:     evidence_id: str,
 164:     evidence_pool_raw: dict[str, Any] | list[Any] | None,
 165: ) -> str | None:
 166:     """Lookup evidence body in evidence_pool.json (Codex iter-2 P2 Q4).
 167: 
 168:     Pipeline-A's persisted field is commonly `direct_quote`, not full_text.
 169:     """
 170:     if evidence_pool_raw is None:
 171:         return None
 172:     sources = (
 173:         evidence_pool_raw.get("sources") if isinstance(evidence_pool_raw, dict)
 174:         else evidence_pool_raw
 175:     )
 176:     if not isinstance(sources, list):
 177:         return None
 178:     for src in sources:
 179:         if not isinstance(src, dict):
 180:             continue
 181:         if src.get("evidence_id") == evidence_id or src.get("source_id") == evidence_id:
 182:             return (
 183:                 src.get("full_text")
 184:                 or src.get("direct_quote")
 185:                 or src.get("snippet")
 186:             )
 187:     return None
 188: 
 189: 
 190: def _parse_iso(value: Any) -> datetime | None:
 191:     if not value:
 192:         return None
 193:     if isinstance(value, datetime):
 194:         return value
 195:     try:
 196:         return datetime.fromisoformat(str(value).replace("Z", "+00:00"))
 197:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 198:         return None
 199: 
 200: 
 201: def build_slice_chain(
 202:     artifact_dir: Path,
 203: ) -> tuple[ScopeDecision, EvidencePool, SliceChainVerifiedReport]:
 204:     """Convert a pipeline-A canonical artifact dir to slice-chain Pydantic models.
 205: 
 206:     Raises:
 207:         FileNotFoundError: artifact_dir missing required canonical files
 208:         SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError: sovereignty cascade leaves no
 209:             non-dropped sections (cannot ship a bundle for this run)
 210:     """
 211:     air = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 212:     manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 213:     evidence_pool_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "evidence_pool.json")
 214: 
 215:     # ─── 1. ScopeDecision ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 216:     decision_id = (
 217:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("decision_id")
 218:         or manifest_raw.get("external_run_id")
 219:         or str(uuid.uuid4())
 220:     )
 221:     scope_class = _derive_scope_class(
 222:         manifest_raw.get("domain"),
 223:         (manifest_raw.get("scope") or {}).get("classification"),
 224:     )
 225:     decision = ScopeDecision(
 226:         decision_id=decision_id,
 227:         status="in_scope",
 228:         scope_class=scope_class,
 229:         ambiguity_axes=[],
 230:         clarifications_needed=[],
 231:         provenance={
 232:             "classifier_layer": "pipeline_a_v30",
 233:             "artifact_dir": str(artifact_dir),
 234:         },
 235:     )
 236: 
 237:     # ─── 2. EvidencePool (sovereignty-filtered) ───────────────────────────
 238:     sources: list[Source] = []
 239:     cleared_evidence_ids: set[str] = set()
 240:     for entry in air.bibliography:
 241:         # Tier-1 is legal-cleared by default; non-T1 requires explicit clearance
 242:         # in evidence_pool.json provenance.legal_cleared = True (Phase 2 hook).
 243:         canonical_tier, raw_tier = _normalize_tier(entry.tier)
 244:         is_legal_cleared = canonical_tier == SourceTier.T1
 245:         if not is_legal_cleared:
 246:             continue  # exclude — sovereignty_guard would reject otherwise
 247:         full_text = _full_text_for_evidence_id(entry.evidence_id, evidence_pool_raw)
 248:         sources.append(Source(
 249:             source_id=entry.evidence_id,
 250:             url=entry.url,
 251:             domain=_url_domain(entry.url),
 252:             tier=canonical_tier,
 253:             title=entry.statement[:200] or "Untitled",
 254:             snippet=entry.statement[:1000] or "n/a",
 255:             full_text_available=full_text is not None,
 256:             full_text=full_text,
 257:             provenance={
 258:                 "legal_cleared": True,
 259:                 "raw_tier": raw_tier,
 260:             },
 261:             retracted=False,
 262:         ))
 263:         cleared_evidence_ids.add(entry.evidence_id)
 264: 
 265:     retrieval_block = manifest_raw.get("retrieval", {}) or {}
 266:     started_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("started_at")) or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
 267:     finished_utc = _parse_iso(retrieval_block.get("finished_at")) or started_utc
 268:     pool = EvidencePool(
 269:         pool_id=retrieval_block.get("pool_id") or str(uuid.uuid4()),
 270:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 271:         sources=sources,
 272:         adequacy=AdequacyVerdict(
 273:             is_adequate=True,
 274:             adequacy_score=1.0,
 275:             failure_reason=None,
 276:         ),
 277:         queries_executed=retrieval_block.get("queries_executed", []) or [],
 278:         retrieval_started_at_utc=started_utc,
 279:         retrieval_finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 280:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 281:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 282:     )
 283: 
 284:     # ─── 3. VerifiedReport (sovereignty cascade) ──────────────────────────
 285:     sections: list[Section] = []
 286:     for air_section in air.verified_report.sections:
 287:         kept: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
 288:         for air_sent in air_section.sentences:
 289:             sc_sent = _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent)
 290:             cited_ids = _evidence_ids_in_tokens(sc_sent.provenance_tokens)
 291:             if not cited_ids or cited_ids.issubset(cleared_evidence_ids):
 292:                 kept.append(sc_sent)
 293:             else:
 294:                 kept.append(_redact_sentence(sc_sent))
 295:         pass_count = sum(1 for s in kept if s.verifier_pass)
 296:         section_status: SectionStatus = (
 297:             "dropped" if pass_count == 0 else "verified"
 298:         )
 299:         sections.append(Section(
 300:             section_id=_slugify(air_section.title) or f"section_{len(sections)}",
 301:             section_title=air_section.title or f"Section {len(sections)}",
 302:             verified_sentences=kept,
 303:             section_verify_pass_rate=pass_count / max(len(kept), 1),
 304:             section_status=section_status,
 305:         ))
 306: 
 307:     non_dropped = [s for s in sections if s.section_status != "dropped"]
 308:     if not non_dropped:
 309:         raise SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError(
 310:             "every section dropped after sovereignty cascade; bundle cannot be assembled"
 311:         )
 312: 
 313:     overall = sum(s.section_verify_pass_rate for s in non_dropped) / len(non_dropped)
 314:     # Codex diff iter-1 P2-001 fix: partial_* runs still have kept sections;
 315:     # they're "success-with-degradation" not "no_verified_sections" aborts.
 316:     # PipelineVerdict Literal accepts success | abort_no_verified_sections;
 317:     # collapse partial_* into "success" since the pipeline did produce kept
 318:     # content (the degradation is recorded on the manifest, not the verdict).
 319:     manifest_status = air.manifest.status or ""
 320:     if manifest_status == "success" or manifest_status.startswith("partial_"):
 321:         pipeline_verdict: PipelineVerdict = "success"
 322:     else:
 323:         pipeline_verdict = "abort_no_verified_sections"
 324:     models_block = manifest_raw.get("models") or {}
 325:     report = SliceChainVerifiedReport(
 326:         report_id=air.manifest.run_id,
 327:         pool_id=pool.pool_id,
 328:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 329:         sections=sections,
 330:         overall_verify_pass_rate=overall,
 331:         pipeline_verdict=pipeline_verdict,
 332:         generator_model=models_block.get("generator") or "unknown",
 333:         evaluator_model=models_block.get("evaluator") or "strict_verify_v1",
 334:         family_segregation_passed=True,
 335:         verifier_pass_threshold=0.4,
 336:         started_at_utc=started_utc,
 337:         finished_at_utc=finished_utc,
 338:         latency_ms=int(retrieval_block.get("latency_ms") or 0),
 339:         cost_usd=float(air.manifest.cost_usd or 0.0),
 340:     )
 341:     return decision, pool, report
 342: 
 343: 
 344: def _air_sentence_to_slice_chain(air_sent: AuditIRSentence) -> VerifiedSentence:
 345:     """AuditIR ReportSentence → slice-chain VerifiedSentence."""
 346:     failure = air_sent.failure_reasons[0] if air_sent.failure_reasons else None
 347:     return VerifiedSentence(
 348:         section_id=_slugify(air_sent.section) or "section",
 349:         sentence_text=air_sent.text or "n/a",
 350:         provenance_tokens=_tokens_to_strings(air_sent.tokens),
 351:         verifier_pass=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 352:         drop_reason=_normalize_drop_reason(failure) if not air_sent.is_verified else None,
 353:         evaluator_agrees=bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 354:         is_synthesis_claim=len(air_sent.tokens) == 0 and bool(air_sent.is_verified),
 355:     )
 356: 
 357: 
 358: def _url_domain(url: str) -> str:
 359:     """Extract host for the Source.domain field. Falls back to 'unknown'."""
 360:     from urllib.parse import urlparse
 361:     try:
 362:         return urlparse(str(url)).netloc or "unknown"
 363:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive: never raise during bridge
 364:         return "unknown"
 365: 
 366: 
 367: def _slugify(text: str) -> str:
 368:     return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", (text or "").lower()).strip("_")[:60]

  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: from typing import Literal
  19: 
  20: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  21: 
  22: 
  23: class SourceSpan(BaseModel):
  24:     """A verbatim span lifted from a cited source document."""
  25: 
  26:     evidence_id: str = Field(..., description="Stable id for this evidence pool member.")
  27:     source_url: str = Field(..., description="Canonical URL to the source.")
  28:     source_tier: Literal["T1", "T2", "T3"] = Field(
  29:         ...,
  30:         description="Source admissibility tier per CLAUDE.md §9 corpus adequacy gate.",
  31:     )
  32:     span_start: int = Field(..., ge=0, description="Inclusive char offset within source body.")
  33:     span_end: int = Field(..., gt=0, description="Exclusive char offset within source body.")
  34:     span_text: str = Field(..., min_length=1, description="Verbatim span text.")
  35: 
  36: 
  37: class VerifiedSentence(BaseModel):
  38:     """A generator sentence that passed strict_verify Local + Global."""
  39: 
  40:     section_id: str
  41:     sentence_text: str
  42:     provenance_tokens: list[str] = Field(
  43:         ...,
  44:         description=(
  45:             "List of [#ev:<evidence_id>:<start>-<end>] tokens per CLAUDE.md "
  46:             "§9.1 invariant 2."
  47:         ),
  48:     )
  49:     verifier_local_pass: bool
  50:     verifier_global_pass: bool
  51:     drop_reason: str | None = Field(
  52:         default=None,
  53:         description=(
  54:             "Null if sentence shipped. Otherwise one of "
  55:             "evidence_id_not_in_pool | span_oob | numeric_mismatch | "
  56:             "content_word_overlap_lt_2 | numeric_consistency_violation | "
  57:             "frame_imbalance | contradiction_unresolved."
  58:         ),
  59:     )

  62: class FrameCoverage(BaseModel):

  65:     frame_id: str
  66:     frame_name: str
  67:     sources_assigned: int
  68:     coverage_percent: float = Field(..., ge=0.0, le=100.0)
  69: 
  70: 
  71: class ContradictionRecord(BaseModel):

  78:     evidence_a: list[str]

  81: 
  82: 
  83: class EvidenceContract(BaseModel):

   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12):
   4: - Migration: RENAME COLUMN status → lifecycle_status (SQLite 3.25+)
   5: - New columns: query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, pipeline_status,
   6:   cost_usd, decision_id (all nullable; backward-compatible)
   7: - New helpers: mark_failed, mark_aborted, set_pipeline_meta
   8: - get_run returns the full RunStatusResponse with new optional fields
   9: 
  10: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): cancellation support.
  11: - New column: cancel_requested (INTEGER 0/1).
  12: - request_cancel: queued → cancelled atomically (T1, instant); in_progress
  13:   → set the cancel flag (T2, cooperative — the worker observes it).
  14: - mark_in_progress is now a compare-and-swap (only transitions a queued,
  15:   not-cancel-requested row) so a queued cancel cannot be overwritten.
  16: - is_cancel_requested / mark_cancelled support the worker's cooperative
  17:   abort path.
  18: 
  19: I-rdy-013 (2026-05-16): 1-concurrent-session enforcement.
  20: - get_active_run: read-side helper — the run currently holding the session.
  21: - insert_run_if_idle: atomic check-and-insert (BEGIN IMMEDIATE) used by
  22:   POST /runs so a 2nd concurrent request cannot start a parallel session.
  23: - init_db serialized by `_INIT_LOCK`; `_connect` sets `busy_timeout`.
  24: 
  25: Default DB path: state/v6_runs.sqlite (gitignored). Override via env
  26: `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB`. WAL mode enabled.
  27: """
  28: 
  29: from __future__ import annotations
  30: 
  31: import json
  32: import os
  33: import sqlite3
  34: import threading
  35: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  36: from typing import Any
  37: 
  38: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  39: 
  40: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
  41: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
  42: 
  43: # Lifecycle states from which a run can no longer transition. Public so the
  44: # /runs/{id}/cancel endpoint shares one definition of "terminal".
  45: TERMINAL_STATUSES = ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")
  46: 
  47: # Columns selected by get_run (single source of truth for both the
  48: # first-attempt and post-migration-retry queries).
  49: _RUN_COLUMNS = (
  50:     "run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
  51:     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
  52:     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id, "
  53:     "cancel_requested"
  54: )
  55: 
  56: # I-rdy-013: lifecycle states that count as an active research session. A run
  57: # in one of these blocks a new POST /runs (1-concurrent-session constraint).
  58: # `completed`, `cancelled`, `failed` are terminal and free the session slot.
  59: _ACTIVE_STATUSES = ("queued", "in_progress")
  60: 
  61: # I-rdy-013: serializes init_db across in-process threads so two concurrent
  62: # first requests cannot collide inside `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema
  63: # migration and raise sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate runs.
  64: _INIT_LOCK = threading.Lock()
  65: 
  66: 
  67: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
  68:     if path is not None:
  69:         return path
  70:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def _now_iso() -> str:
  74:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  75: 
  76: 
  77: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  78:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  79:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  80:     if parent:
  81:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  82:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  83:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  84:     # I-rdy-013: a concurrent writer waits up to 5s for the write lock
  85:     # instead of raising SQLITE_BUSY immediately (the issue's "no crash").
  86:     conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000")
  87:     return conn
  88: 
  89: 
  90: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  91:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  92: 
  93:     1. Create base table if absent.
  94:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  95:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  96:        SQLite 3.34+).
  97:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a / I-rdy-011 field if missing.
  98:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  99:     """
 100:     conn.execute(
 101:         """
 102:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
 103:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 104:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
 105:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
 106:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
 107:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
 108:             started_at TEXT,
 109:             finished_at TEXT,
 110:             result_json TEXT,
 111:             error_json TEXT
 112:         )
 113:         """
 114:     )
 115:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
 116:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
 117:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
 118:         cols.discard("status")
 119:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
 120:     for col_name, col_type in {
 121:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
 122:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
 123:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
 124:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
 125:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
 126:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
 127:         "cancel_requested": "INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0",
 128:     }.items():
 129:         if col_name not in cols:
 130:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
 131:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
 132:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
 133: 
 134: 
 135: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
 136:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent.
 137: 
 138:     I-rdy-013: serialized by `_INIT_LOCK` so two concurrent first requests
 139:     (FastAPI worker threads, one process) cannot collide inside
 140:     `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema migration and raise
 141:     sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate is reached.
 142:     """
 143:     with _INIT_LOCK:
 144:         conn = _connect(path)
 145:         try:
 146:             conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
 147:             _migrate_schema(conn)
 148:             conn.commit()
 149:         finally:
 150:             conn.close()
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def insert_run(run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 154:     """Insert a new row with lifecycle_status='queued'. Raises IntegrityError on duplicate.
 155: 
 156:     Unconditional primitive — does NOT enforce the 1-concurrent-session
 157:     constraint. POST /runs uses `insert_run_if_idle`; this remains for test
 158:     fixtures and any caller that deliberately wants an unconditional insert.
 159:     """
 160:     init_db(path)
 161:     conn = _connect(path)
 162:     try:
 163:         conn.execute(
 164:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 165:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 166:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 167:         )
 168:         conn.commit()
 169:     finally:
 170:         conn.close()
 171: 
 172: 
 173: def insert_run_if_idle(
 174:     run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None
 175: ) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 176:     """Atomically insert a new queued run IFF no run is currently active.
 177: 
 178:     I-rdy-013 (1-concurrent-session enforcement): the check-for-active and
 179:     the INSERT run inside one `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` transaction, so two
 180:     concurrent POST /runs cannot both pass the check. `BEGIN IMMEDIATE`
 181:     takes the write lock up-front; the 2nd writer blocks on it (up to the
 182:     `busy_timeout`) until the 1st commits, then sees the inserted row.
 183: 
 184:     Returns None when the run was inserted; returns the blocking active
 185:     RunStatusResponse when rejected (caller raises HTTP 409).
 186:     """
 187:     init_db(path)
 188:     placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in _ACTIVE_STATUSES)
 189:     conn = _connect(path)
 190:     conn.isolation_level = None  # manual transaction control
 191:     try:
 192:         conn.execute("BEGIN IMMEDIATE")
 193:         row = conn.execute(
 194:             f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 195:             f"WHERE lifecycle_status IN ({placeholders}) "
 196:             "ORDER BY queued_at LIMIT 1",
 197:             _ACTIVE_STATUSES,
 198:         ).fetchone()
 199:         if row is not None:
 200:             conn.execute("ROLLBACK")
 201:             return _row_to_response(row)
 202:         conn.execute(
 203:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 204:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 205:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 206:         )
 207:         conn.execute("COMMIT")
 208:         return None
 209:     finally:
 210:         conn.close()
 211: 
 212: 
 213: def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 214:     """Transition queued → in_progress IFF the run is not cancel-requested.
 215: 
 216:     I-rdy-011: compare-and-swap. The `WHERE lifecycle_status='queued' AND
 217:     cancel_requested=0` guard means a queued cancel that already flipped the
 218:     row to 'cancelled' cannot be overwritten by a worker picking the run up.
 219: 
 220:     Returns True iff the row transitioned; False means the run was cancelled
 221:     (or already past 'queued') and the caller must not run the pipeline.
 222:     """
 223:     conn = _connect(path)
 224:     try:
 225:         cur = conn.execute(
 226:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? "
 227:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued' AND cancel_requested=0",
 228:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 229:         )
 230:         conn.commit()
 231:         return cur.rowcount > 0
 232:     finally:
 233:         conn.close()
 234: 
 235: 
 236: def request_cancel(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> str | None:
 237:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011).
 238: 
 239:     - queued run → atomically transitioned to terminal 'cancelled' (T1,
 240:       instant — the worker's mark_in_progress CAS will then no-op).
 241:     - in_progress run → cancel_requested flag set; lifecycle stays
 242:       'in_progress' until the worker observes the flag at a pipeline stage
 243:       boundary and calls mark_cancelled (T2, cooperative).
 244: 
 245:     Returns the resulting lifecycle_status ('cancelled' or 'in_progress'),
 246:     or None if the run does not exist or is already terminal.
 247:     """
 248:     conn = _connect(path)
 249:     try:
 250:         # T1: queued → cancelled, atomically.
 251:         cur = conn.execute(
 252:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 253:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued'",
 254:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 255:         )
 256:         if cur.rowcount > 0:
 257:             conn.commit()
 258:             return "cancelled"
 259:         # T2: in_progress → set the flag for the worker to observe.
 260:         cur = conn.execute(
 261:             "UPDATE runs SET cancel_requested=1 "
 262:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='in_progress'",
 263:             (run_id,),
 264:         )
 265:         conn.commit()
 266:         return "in_progress" if cur.rowcount > 0 else None
 267:     finally:
 268:         conn.close()
 269: 
 270: 
 271: def is_cancel_requested(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 272:     """True iff a cancellation has been requested for the run.
 273: 
 274:     Best-effort: a missing run / missing table returns False.
 275:     """
 276:     conn = _connect(path)
 277:     try:
 278:         try:
 279:             row = conn.execute(
 280:                 "SELECT cancel_requested FROM runs WHERE run_id=?", (run_id,)
 281:             ).fetchone()
 282:         except sqlite3.OperationalError:
 283:             return False
 284:         return bool(row["cancel_requested"]) if row is not None else False
 285:     finally:
 286:         conn.close()
 287: 
 288: 
 289: def mark_cancelled(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 290:     """Terminal transition → lifecycle_status='cancelled' + finished_at.
 291: 
 292:     Used by the worker when it observes cancel_requested at a pipeline
 293:     stage boundary (cooperative T2 abort), and as the actor's mapping for a
 294:     pipeline-A manifest with status 'cancelled'.
 295:     """
 296:     conn = _connect(path)
 297:     try:
 298:         conn.execute(
 299:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 300:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
 301:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 302:         )
 303:         conn.commit()
 304:     finally:
 305:         conn.close()
 306: 
 307: 
 308: def set_pipeline_meta(
 309:     run_id: str,
 310:     *,
 311:     query_slug: str | None = None,
 312:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None,
 313:     artifact_dir: str | None = None,
 314:     decision_id: str | None = None,
 315:     path: str | None = None,
 316: ) -> None:
 317:     """Set pipeline-A metadata after the actor learns the slug/dir.
 318: 
 319:     Independent of lifecycle transition so the actor can record meta as
 320:     soon as pipeline-A starts, before the run completes.
 321:     """
 322:     conn = _connect(path)
 323:     try:
 324:         conn.execute(
 325:             "UPDATE runs SET query_slug=COALESCE(?, query_slug), "
 326:             "manifest_run_id=COALESCE(?, manifest_run_id), "
 327:             "artifact_dir=COALESCE(?, artifact_dir), "
 328:             "decision_id=COALESCE(?, decision_id) WHERE run_id=?",
 329:             (query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, decision_id, run_id),
 330:         )
 331:         conn.commit()
 332:     finally:
 333:         conn.close()
 334:

 336: def mark_completed(
 337:     run_id: str,
 338:     result: dict[str, Any],
 339:     *,
 340:     pipeline_status: str = "success",
 341:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
 342:     path: str | None = None,
 343: ) -> None:
 344:     """Transition in_progress → completed; set finished_at + result_json + pipeline_status + cost_usd."""
 345:     conn = _connect(path)
 346:     try:
 347:         conn.execute(
 348:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, result_json=?, "
 349:             "pipeline_status=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
 350:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(result, sort_keys=True), pipeline_status, cost_usd, run_id),
 351:         )
 352:         conn.commit()
 353:     finally:
 354:         conn.close()

 356: 
 357: def mark_aborted(
 358:     run_id: str,
 359:     *,
 360:     pipeline_status: str,
 361:     abort_reason: str,
 362:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
 363:     path: str | None = None,
 364: ) -> None:
 365:     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
 366: 
 367:     Per CLAUDE.md §9.3, abort_* are pipeline verdicts (not errors). The run
 368:     completed operationally; the pipeline-A logic chose to halt at a gate.
 369:     """
 370:     conn = _connect(path)
 371:     try:
 372:         conn.execute(
 373:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, "
 374:             "pipeline_status=?, error_json=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
 375:             (
 376:                 _now_iso(),
 377:                 pipeline_status,
 378:                 json.dumps({"abort_reason": abort_reason}, sort_keys=True),
 379:                 cost_usd,
 380:                 run_id,
 381:             ),
 382:         )
 383:         conn.commit()
 384:     finally:
 385:         conn.close()
 386: 
 387: 
 388: def mark_failed(
 389:     run_id: str,
 390:     error: str,
 391:     *,
 392:     path: str | None = None,
 393:     uploaded_documents_used: int | None = None,
 394:     uploaded_documents_blocked: int | None = None,
 395: ) -> None:
 396:     """Operational failure (exception, missing manifest, unknown status, etc).
 397: 
 398:     Distinct from mark_aborted: failures are unplanned (exception or invariant
 399:     violation); aborts are planned (pipeline_status='abort_*' written by
 400:     pipeline-A at a gate).
 401: 
 402:     I-cd-018 (#628): optional `uploaded_documents_used` +
 403:     `uploaded_documents_blocked` flow into `error_json` so the error-path
 404:     observability mirrors the success-path INFO log (actors.py:146-151).
 405:     Keys are present in error_json only when caller passes them.
 406:     """
 407:     error_payload: dict[str, object] = {"error": error}
 408:     if uploaded_documents_used is not None:
 409:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_used"] = uploaded_documents_used
 410:     if uploaded_documents_blocked is not None:
 411:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_blocked"] = uploaded_documents_blocked
 412:     conn = _connect(path)
 413:     try:
 414:         conn.execute(
 415:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='failed', finished_at=?, "
 416:             "pipeline_status='error_unexpected', error_json=? WHERE run_id=?",
 417:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(error_payload, sort_keys=True), run_id),
 418:         )
 419:         conn.commit()
 420:     finally:
 421:         conn.close()
 422: 
 423: 
 424: def _row_to_response(row: sqlite3.Row) -> RunStatusResponse:
 425:     return RunStatusResponse(
 426:         run_id=row["run_id"],
 427:         template=row["template"],
 428:         question=row["question"],
 429:         lifecycle_status=row["lifecycle_status"],
 430:         pipeline_status=row["pipeline_status"],
 431:         queued_at=row["queued_at"],
 432:         started_at=row["started_at"],
 433:         finished_at=row["finished_at"],
 434:         result_json=row["result_json"],
 435:         error_json=row["error_json"],
 436:         query_slug=row["query_slug"],
 437:         manifest_run_id=row["manifest_run_id"],
 438:         artifact_dir=row["artifact_dir"],
 439:         cost_usd=row["cost_usd"],
 440:         decision_id=row["decision_id"],
 441:         cancel_requested=bool(row["cancel_requested"]),
 442:     )

 445: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 446:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 447: 
 448:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 449:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 450:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 451:     contract.
 452: 
 453:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 454:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 455:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 456:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 457:     """
 458:     conn = _connect(path)
 459:     try:
 460:         try:
 461:             row = conn.execute(
 462:                 f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 463:                 (run_id,),
 464:             ).fetchone()
 465:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 466:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 467:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 468:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 469:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 470:             # missing-row.
 471:             if "no such table" in msg:
 472:                 return None
 473:             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
 474:             if "no such column" in msg:
 475:                 conn.close()
 476:                 init_db(path)
 477:                 conn = _connect(path)
 478:                 row = conn.execute(
 479:                     f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 480:                     (run_id,),
 481:                 ).fetchone()
 482:             else:
 483:                 raise
 484:     finally:
 485:         conn.close()
 486:     if row is None:
 487:         return None
 488:     return _row_to_response(row)
 489: 
 490: 
 491: def get_active_run(*, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 492:     """Return the oldest run still queued or in_progress, else None.
 493: 
 494:     I-rdy-013: read-side helper for the 1-concurrent-session constraint —
 495:     the run currently holding the session slot. At most one run is active
 496:     once `insert_run_if_idle` gates all inserts; the `ORDER BY queued_at`
 497:     is defensive (oldest first) for any pre-gate legacy rows.
 498: 
 499:     Defensive against a missing/legacy table, mirroring `get_run`.
 500:     """
 501:     placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in _ACTIVE_STATUSES)
 502:     query = (
 503:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 504:         f"WHERE lifecycle_status IN ({placeholders}) "
 505:         "ORDER BY queued_at LIMIT 1"
 506:     )
 507:     conn = _connect(path)
 508:     try:
 509:         try:
 510:             row = conn.execute(query, _ACTIVE_STATUSES).fetchone()
 511:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 512:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 513:             if "no such table" in msg:
 514:                 return None
 515:             if "no such column" in msg:
 516:                 conn.close()
 517:                 init_db(path)
 518:                 conn = _connect(path)
 519:                 row = conn.execute(query, _ACTIVE_STATUSES).fetchone()
 520:             else:
 521:                 raise
 522:     finally:
 523:         conn.close()
 524:     return None if row is None else _row_to_response(row)
 525: 
 526: 
 527: def list_completed_runs_by_query_slug(
 528:     query_slug: str, *, path: str | None = None
 529: ) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
 530:     """List completed runs sharing a query_slug ordered by finished_at ASC.
 531: 
 532:     I-cd-017 (#627): pin-replay timeseries source. Uses the existing
 533:     `idx_runs_query_slug` index. Returns `[]` (not None) when no rows
 534:     match — callers distinguish "anchor run exists but no completed
 535:     siblings" from "anchor run unknown" via get_run() before calling.
 536: 
 537:     Defensive against missing-table / legacy-schema like get_run.
 538:     """
 539:     query = (
 540:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 541:         "WHERE query_slug=? AND lifecycle_status='completed' "
 542:         "ORDER BY finished_at ASC"
 543:     )
 544:     conn = _connect(path)
 545:     try:
 546:         try:
 547:             rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
 548:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 549:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 550:             if "no such table" in msg:
 551:                 return []
 552:             if "no such column" in msg:
 553:                 conn.close()
 554:                 init_db(path)
 555:                 conn = _connect(path)
 556:                 rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
 557:             else:
 558:                 raise
 559:     finally:
 560:         conn.close()
 561:     return [_row_to_response(row) for row in rows]

+"""I-cd-680 — bridge a real pipeline-A artifact_dir to a typed EvidenceContract.
+
+Reuses `build_slice_chain` (I-arch-001d, the same path `GET /runs/{id}/
+bundle.tar.gz` already proves on real runs) and maps the slice-chain into the
+`EvidenceContract` v1.0 schema that the follow-up (#542) and compare (#543)
+endpoints consume.
+
+Scope (Codex Option B, 2026-05-20): real-run RESOLUTION only. We do NOT
+synthesize rich source-document char offsets — pipeline-A does not record
+them. `SourceSpan.span_start`/`span_end` are the truthful 0..len(span_text)
+offsets of the recorded evidence text within ITSELF (the recorded quote IS
+the span). Rich offsets into the original source body are the deferred
+Phase-2 capability (#710), NOT fabricated here (LAW II).
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_slice_chain import build_slice_chain
+from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import (
+    ContradictionRecord,
+    EvidenceContract,
+    SourceSpan,
+    VerifiedSentence,
+)
+
+
+def _read_contradictions(artifact_dir: Path) -> list[ContradictionRecord]:
+    """Load contradictions.json if present. Real pipeline-A runs write a list
+    of contradiction records; absent/empty → no contradictions."""
+    path = artifact_dir / "contradictions.json"
+    if not path.exists():
+        return []
+    try:
+        raw = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):
+        return []
+    records: list[ContradictionRecord] = []
+    items = raw if isinstance(raw, list) else raw.get("contradictions", [])
+    for i, item in enumerate(items if isinstance(items, list) else []):
+        if not isinstance(item, dict):
+            continue
+        try:
+            records.append(
+                ContradictionRecord(
+                    contradiction_id=str(item.get("contradiction_id") or f"c{i}"),
+                    section_id=str(item.get("section_id") or "unknown"),
+                    claim_a=str(item.get("claim_a") or ""),
+                    claim_b=str(item.get("claim_b") or ""),
+                    evidence_a=[str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_a") or [])],
+                    evidence_b=[str(x) for x in (item.get("evidence_b") or [])],
+                    resolution=item.get("resolution")
+                    if item.get("resolution")
+                    in ("unresolved", "claim_a_preferred", "claim_b_preferred", "noted_both")
+                    else "noted_both",
+                )
+            )
+        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — a malformed record is skipped, not fatal
+            continue
+    return records
+
+
+def build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
+    artifact_dir: Path,
+    *,
+    run_id: str,
+    template: str,
+    question: str,
+    queued_at: str,
+    finished_at: str,
+    pipeline_status: str,
+) -> EvidenceContract:
+    """Synthesize a fully-valid EvidenceContract from a REAL artifact_dir.
+
+    Run metadata (run_id/template/question/timestamps/status) is supplied by
+    the caller from run_store (the authoritative source); the evidence + the
+    verified sentences come from the slice-chain.
+
+    Raises FileNotFoundError / SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError from
+    build_slice_chain — the caller maps these to 404 / 422.
+    """
+    _decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
+
+    evidence_pool: list[SourceSpan] = []
+    for src in pool.sources:
+        # The recorded evidence text. build_slice_chain only admits T1
+        # legal-cleared sources, so source_tier is within SourceSpan's
+        # T1/T2/T3 Literal.
+        span_text = src.full_text or src.snippet or src.title or "n/a"
+        evidence_pool.append(
+            SourceSpan(
+                evidence_id=src.source_id,
+                source_url=str(src.url),
+                source_tier=src.tier.value,
+                # Truthful self-offset of the recorded span; rich
+                # source-document offsets are deferred to #710.
+                span_start=0,
+                span_end=len(span_text),
+                span_text=span_text,
+            )
+        )
+
+    verified_sentences: list[VerifiedSentence] = []
+    for section in report.sections:
+        for sent in section.verified_sentences:
+            verified_sentences.append(
+                VerifiedSentence(
+                    section_id=sent.section_id,
+                    sentence_text=sent.sentence_text,
+                    provenance_tokens=list(sent.provenance_tokens),
+                    # The slice-chain records a single verifier_pass (Local AND
+                    # Global must both hold for a sentence to pass strict_verify),
+                    # so it maps to both EvidenceContract flags.
+                    verifier_local_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
+                    verifier_global_pass=sent.verifier_pass,
+                    drop_reason=sent.drop_reason,
+                )
+            )
+
+    return EvidenceContract(
+        run_id=run_id,
+        template=template,
+        question=question,
+        queued_at=queued_at,
+        finished_at=finished_at,
+        pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
+        evidence_pool=evidence_pool,
+        verified_sentences=verified_sentences,
+        frame_coverage=[],
+        contradictions=_read_contradictions(artifact_dir),
+        cost_usd=float(report.cost_usd or 0.0),
+        generator_model=report.generator_model,
+        verifier_model=report.evaluator_model,
+        family_segregation_passed=report.family_segregation_passed,
+    )

+"""I-cd-680 — build_evidence_contract_from_artifact coverage (Codex Option B).
+
+Reuses the synthetic AuditIR-shape artifact builder from the slice-chain
+tests. Verifies a REAL artifact_dir maps to a valid EvidenceContract with
+NO fabricated source-document offsets (span_start=0, span_end=len of the
+recorded span text — the truthful self-offset; rich offsets are deferred
+to #710).
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import pytest
+
+from polaris_v6.api.artifact_to_evidence_contract import (
+    build_evidence_contract_from_artifact,
+)
+from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import EvidenceContract
+from tests.polaris_v6.api.test_artifact_to_slice_chain import (
+    _write_synthetic_artifact_dir,
+)
+
+
+def _build(tmp_path, **kw) -> EvidenceContract:
+    artifact_dir = _write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path, **kw)
+    return build_evidence_contract_from_artifact(
+        artifact_dir,
+        run_id="real_run_001",
+        template="ai_sovereignty",
+        question="What sovereign compute does Canada have?",
+        queued_at="2026-05-20T00:00:00+00:00",
+        finished_at="2026-05-20T00:10:00+00:00",
+        pipeline_status="success",
+    )
+
+
+def test_real_artifact_builds_valid_evidence_contract(tmp_path):
+    ec = _build(tmp_path)
+    assert isinstance(ec, EvidenceContract)
+    assert ec.run_id == "real_run_001"
+    assert ec.template == "ai_sovereignty"
+    assert ec.contract_version == "1.0"
+    # Run metadata threaded from the caller (run_store), not the artifact.
+    assert ec.question.startswith("What sovereign")
+    assert ec.pipeline_status == "success"
+
+
+def test_evidence_pool_offsets_are_truthful_self_offsets(tmp_path):
+    """No fabricated source-document offsets (Codex Option B). Each SourceSpan
+    has span_start=0 and span_end=len(span_text) — the recorded span IS the
+    text; rich offsets into the original source body are deferred (#710)."""
+    ec = _build(tmp_path)
+    assert ec.evidence_pool, "expected at least one cleared (T1) source"
+    for span in ec.evidence_pool:
+        assert span.span_start == 0
+        assert span.span_end == len(span.span_text)
+        assert span.span_text  # non-empty
+        assert span.source_tier in ("T1", "T2", "T3")
+
+
+def test_verified_sentences_carry_provenance(tmp_path):
+    ec = _build(tmp_path)
+    assert ec.verified_sentences, "expected verified sentences from the report"
+    for s in ec.verified_sentences:
+        assert s.section_id
+        assert s.sentence_text
+        # provenance_tokens is a list[str] mapped straight from the slice-chain.
+        assert isinstance(s.provenance_tokens, list)
+
+
+def test_models_and_cost_threaded_from_slice_chain(tmp_path):
+    ec = _build(tmp_path, cost_usd=1.23)
+    assert ec.cost_usd == pytest.approx(1.23)
+    assert ec.generator_model  # non-empty (from manifest models block / default)
+    assert ec.verifier_model
+    assert isinstance(ec.family_segregation_passed, bool)

 succeeded in 1804ms:
   1: """Phase 3 substrate: deterministic stub follow-up agent.
   2: 
   3: The real Phase 3 implementation calls the verifier model with a
   4: prompt that constrains it to the parent run's evidence pool. Phase 0
   5: ships this stub to lock the contract: takes a parent EvidenceContract
   6: + a question, returns a FollowUpAnswer with status determined by simple
   7: keyword overlap. This is enough for the F11 endpoint contract test.
   8: """
   9: 
  10: from __future__ import annotations
  11: 
  12: import re
  13: 
  14: from polaris_v6.followup.schema import FollowUpAnswer
  15: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import EvidenceContract
  16: 
  17: _TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"[a-z0-9]+")
  18: 
  19: 
  20: def _tokens(text: str) -> set[str]:
  21:     return {t for t in _TOKEN_RE.findall(text.lower()) if len(t) > 2}
  22: 
  23: 
  24: def answer_followup(
  25:     *,
  26:     parent: EvidenceContract,
  27:     question: str,
  28: ) -> FollowUpAnswer:
  29:     q_tokens = _tokens(question)
  30:     if not q_tokens:
  31:         return FollowUpAnswer(
  32:             parent_run_id=parent.run_id,
  33:             question=question,
  34:             status="evidence_insufficient",
  35:             rationale="Question contains no content tokens after normalization.",
  36:         )
  37: 
  38:     pool_hits: list[tuple[str, int]] = []
  39:     for span in parent.evidence_pool:
  40:         span_tokens = _tokens(span.span_text)
  41:         overlap = len(q_tokens & span_tokens)
  42:         if overlap > 0:
  43:             pool_hits.append((span.evidence_id, overlap))
  44: 
  45:     if not pool_hits:
  46:         return FollowUpAnswer(
  47:             parent_run_id=parent.run_id,
  48:             question=question,
  49:             status="out_of_scope",
  50:             rationale=(
  51:                 "No tokens in the question overlap with the parent run's "
  52:                 "evidence pool. Start a new run to broaden retrieval."
  53:             ),
  54:         )
  55: 
  56:     pool_hits.sort(key=lambda h: -h[1])
  57:     used_ids = [eid for eid, _ in pool_hits[:3]]
  58: 
  59:     if len(used_ids) < 1:
  60:         return FollowUpAnswer(
  61:             parent_run_id=parent.run_id,
  62:             question=question,
  63:             status="evidence_insufficient",
  64:             rationale="Insufficient supporting evidence after deduplication.",
  65:             used_evidence_ids=[],
  66:         )
  67: 
  68:     spans_by_id = {s.evidence_id: s for s in parent.evidence_pool}
  69:     tokens = []
  70:     for ev_id in used_ids:
  71:         span = spans_by_id[ev_id]
  72:         tokens.append(f"[#ev:{ev_id}:{span.span_start}-{span.span_end}]")
  73: 
  74:     sentences = [
  75:         spans_by_id[eid].span_text + f" {tokens[i]}"
  76:         for i, eid in enumerate(used_ids)
  77:     ]
  78:     answer_text = " ".join(sentences)
  79: 
  80:     return FollowUpAnswer(
  81:         parent_run_id=parent.run_id,
  82:         question=question,
  83:         status="answered",
  84:         answer_text=answer_text,
  85:         used_evidence_ids=used_ids,
  86:         provenance_tokens=tokens,
  87:         rationale=(
  88:             f"Question shares content tokens with {len(pool_hits)} pool members; "
  89:             f"top-{len(used_ids)} used as supporting evidence."
  90:         ),
  91:     )

 succeeded in 2018ms:
   1: """Compare two EvidenceContract bundles side-by-side."""
   2: 
   3: from __future__ import annotations
   4: 
   5: from dataclasses import dataclass
   6: 
   7: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import EvidenceContract
   8: 
   9: 
  10: @dataclass
  11: class ReportComparison:
  12:     left_run_id: str
  13:     right_run_id: str
  14:     same_template: bool
  15:     same_question: bool
  16:     shared_evidence_ids: list[str]
  17:     only_left_evidence_ids: list[str]
  18:     only_right_evidence_ids: list[str]
  19:     shared_evidence_pct: float  # |shared| / |left ∪ right|
  20:     frame_coverage_overlap: list[str]  # frame_ids present in both
  21:     only_left_frames: list[str]
  22:     only_right_frames: list[str]
  23:     left_contradictions: int
  24:     right_contradictions: int
  25:     pipeline_status_match: bool
  26:     family_segregation_both_pass: bool
  27: 
  28: 
  29: def compare_reports(left: EvidenceContract, right: EvidenceContract) -> ReportComparison:
  30:     if left.run_id == right.run_id:
  31:         raise ValueError("compare_reports requires two distinct runs")
  32: 
  33:     left_ev = {s.evidence_id for s in left.evidence_pool}
  34:     right_ev = {s.evidence_id for s in right.evidence_pool}
  35:     shared = sorted(left_ev & right_ev)
  36:     union = left_ev | right_ev
  37:     shared_pct = len(shared) / len(union) if union else 0.0
  38: 
  39:     left_frames = {f.frame_id for f in left.frame_coverage}
  40:     right_frames = {f.frame_id for f in right.frame_coverage}
  41:     frame_overlap = sorted(left_frames & right_frames)
  42: 
  43:     return ReportComparison(
  44:         left_run_id=left.run_id,
  45:         right_run_id=right.run_id,
  46:         same_template=left.template == right.template,
  47:         same_question=left.question.strip() == right.question.strip(),
  48:         shared_evidence_ids=shared,
  49:         only_left_evidence_ids=sorted(left_ev - right_ev),
  50:         only_right_evidence_ids=sorted(right_ev - left_ev),
  51:         shared_evidence_pct=shared_pct,
  52:         frame_coverage_overlap=frame_overlap,
  53:         only_left_frames=sorted(left_frames - right_frames),
  54:         only_right_frames=sorted(right_frames - left_frames),
  55:         left_contradictions=len(left.contradictions),
  56:         right_contradictions=len(right.contradictions),
  57:         pipeline_status_match=left.pipeline_status == right.pipeline_status,
  58:         family_segregation_both_pass=(
  59:             left.family_segregation_passed and right.family_segregation_passed
  60:         ),
  61:     )
