   1: """Build chart specs from an EvidenceContract bundle.
   2: 
   3: Bridges the existing spec_builder + bundle endpoints. Each chart type
   4: extracts the right slice of the bundle (verified sentences, contradictions,
   5: or per-source numbers) and feeds it to the matching builder.
   6: 
   7: Phase 0/1 stub: deterministic mapping from bundle structure to chart
   8: inputs. Phase 2B will swap in LLM-extracted numeric values when we have
   9: real-pipeline data with per-source structured numerics.
  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from polaris_v6.charts.spec_builder import (
  17:     ComparisonRow,
  18:     ForestPlotPoint,
  19:     TimelinePoint,
  20:     build_comparison_table,
  21:     build_forest_plot,
  22:     build_timeline,
  23: )
  24: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import EvidenceContract
  25: 
  26: ChartType = Literal["forest_plot", "comparison_table", "timeline"]
  27: 
  28: 
  29: def chart_from_bundle(*, bundle: EvidenceContract, chart_type: ChartType) -> dict:
  30:     """Generate a chart spec from a bundle.
  31: 
  32:     For Phase 0, the chart is a deterministic synthetic mapping:
  33:     - forest_plot: each contradiction → one point at estimate=0 with
  34:       ci_low/ci_high reflecting claim_a vs claim_b spread
  35:     - comparison_table: each frame_coverage → one bar per frame with
  36:       coverage_percent value
  37:     - timeline: each verified_sentence → one point ordered by section
  38:     """
  39:     if chart_type == "forest_plot":
  40:         if not bundle.contradictions:
  41:             return build_forest_plot(
  42:                 title=f"Frame coverage for {bundle.template}",
  43:                 points=[
  44:                     ForestPlotPoint(
  45:                         label=f.frame_name[:40],
  46:                         estimate=f.coverage_percent / 100.0,
  47:                         ci_low=max(0.0, (f.coverage_percent - 5) / 100.0),
  48:                         ci_high=min(1.0, (f.coverage_percent + 5) / 100.0),
  49:                         evidence_id=f.frame_id,
  50:                     )
  51:                     for f in bundle.frame_coverage
  52:                 ]
  53:                 or [
  54:                     ForestPlotPoint(
  55:                         label="(no frames)",
  56:                         estimate=0.0,
  57:                         ci_low=0.0,
  58:                         ci_high=0.0,
  59:                         evidence_id="placeholder",
  60:                     )
  61:                 ],
  62:             )
  63:         points = []
  64:         for c in bundle.contradictions:
  65:             evidence_a_id = c.evidence_a[0] if c.evidence_a else "?"
  66:             points.append(
  67:                 ForestPlotPoint(
  68:                     label=c.contradiction_id,
  69:                     estimate=0.0,
  70:                     ci_low=-1.0,
  71:                     ci_high=1.0,
  72:                     evidence_id=evidence_a_id,
  73:                 )
  74:             )
  75:         return build_forest_plot(
  76:             title=f"Contradictions in {bundle.template} run", points=points
  77:         )
  78: 
  79:     if chart_type == "comparison_table":
  80:         if not bundle.frame_coverage:
  81:             return build_comparison_table(
  82:                 title=f"{bundle.template} run — sources by tier",
  83:                 rows=[
  84:                     ComparisonRow(
  85:                         entity=f"tier {span.source_tier}",
  86:                         metric="span_chars",
  87:                         value=float(span.span_end - span.span_start),
  88:                         evidence_id=span.evidence_id,
  89:                     )
  90:                     for span in bundle.evidence_pool
  91:                 ]
  92:                 or [
  93:                     ComparisonRow(
  94:                         entity="(empty pool)",
  95:                         metric="-",
  96:                         value=0.0,
  97:                         evidence_id="placeholder",
  98:                     )
  99:                 ],
 100:             )
 101:         return build_comparison_table(
 102:             title=f"Frame coverage — {bundle.template}",
 103:             rows=[
 104:                 ComparisonRow(
 105:                     entity=f.frame_name[:40],
 106:                     metric="coverage_pct",
 107:                     value=f.coverage_percent,
 108:                     evidence_id=f.frame_id,
 109:                 )
 110:                 for f in bundle.frame_coverage
 111:             ],
 112:         )
 113: 
 114:     if chart_type == "timeline":
 115:         if not bundle.verified_sentences:
 116:             return build_timeline(
 117:                 title=f"{bundle.template} run timeline",
 118:                 points=[
 119:                     TimelinePoint(
 120:                         period="2026-Q2",
 121:                         value=0.0,
 122:                         series="(no sentences)",
 123:                         evidence_id="placeholder",
 124:                     )
 125:                 ],
 126:                 period_kind="quarter",
 127:             )
 128:         points = []
 129:         for idx, s in enumerate(bundle.verified_sentences):
 130:             ev_id = (
 131:                 s.provenance_tokens[0].split(":")[1]
 132:                 if s.provenance_tokens
 133:                 else "unknown"
 134:             )
 135:             points.append(
 136:                 TimelinePoint(
 137:                     period=f"step-{idx + 1:02d}",
 138:                     value=float(idx + 1),
 139:                     series=s.section_id,
 140:                     evidence_id=ev_id,
 141:                 )
 142:             )
 143:         return build_timeline(
 144:             title=f"{bundle.template} verified-sentence timeline",
 145:             points=points,
 146:             period_kind="quarter",
 147:         )
 148: 
 149:     raise ValueError(f"unknown chart_type: {chart_type}")

 succeeded in 1880ms:
   1: """Load a V30 Phase-2 run artifact directory into a canonical AuditIR object.
   2: 
   3: The AuditIR is the single source of truth for the Evidence Inspector and
   4: all derivative renderers. It joins:
   5: - manifest.json (run metadata, frame_coverage_report, corpus tier fractions,
   6:   evaluator gate, v30 warnings, retrieval stats)
   7: - report.md (the rendered markdown report with [N] inline citations)
   8: - bibliography.json (the [N] -> evidence_id -> source mapping)
   9: - contradictions.json (the 14 tier-labeled disagreement clusters with severity)
  10: - verification_details.json (per-section sentences + evidence-span tokens —
  11:   this is the foundation for Evidence Inspector View 1 click-to-inspect)
  12: 
  13: into a single immutable object with lookup methods.
  14: 
  15: Per FINAL_PLAN.md (jointly Claude+Codex agreed):
  16: - The audit graph IR is canonical (NOT the report)
  17: - Evidence Inspector is the primary renderer
  18: - All other outputs are derivative projections with back-links to claim IDs
  19: 
  20: Fail-loud semantics: missing or malformed required schema blocks raise
  21: loudly. There is no silent zero-fill on canonical structures. This is the
  22: audit-grade discipline applied to the IR itself.
  23: """
  24: 
  25: from __future__ import annotations
  26: 
  27: import json
  28: from dataclasses import dataclass
  29: from pathlib import Path
  30: from types import MappingProxyType
  31: from typing import Any, Mapping
  32: 
  33: # Bumped on schema-breaking changes. Renderers should check this and refuse
  34: # to render IR they don't know how to project.
  35: IR_SCHEMA_VERSION = "1.0.0"
  36:

 162: @dataclass(frozen=True)
 163: class FrameCoverageEntry:
 164:     """One contract-slot entity in the frame coverage report.
 165: 
 166:     Includes section / slot_id / subsection_title (back-link into report
 167:     structure) and min_fields_for_completion / human_curated_provenance
 168:     (operator-completion workflow inputs).
 169:     """
 170: 
 171:     entity_id: str
 172:     entity_type: str
 173:     section: str
 174:     slot_id: str
 175:     subsection_title: str
 176:     status: str
 177:     doi: str | None
 178:     pmid: str | None
 179:     failure_reason: str | None
 180:     available_artifacts: tuple[str, ...]
 430:     def get_bibliography_by_num(self, num: int) -> BibliographyEntry | None:
 431:         for entry in self.bibliography:
 432:             if entry.num == num:
 433:                 return entry
 434:         return None
 435: 
 436:     def get_bibliography_by_evidence_id(
 437:         self, evidence_id: str
 438:     ) -> BibliographyEntry | None:
 439:         for entry in self.bibliography:
 440:             if entry.evidence_id == evidence_id:
 441:                 return entry
 442:         return None
 443: 
 444:     def get_contradictions_for_evidence(
 445:         self, evidence_id: str
 446:     ) -> tuple[ContradictionCluster, ...]:
 447:         out = []
 448:         for cluster in self.contradictions:
 449:             if any(c.evidence_id == evidence_id for c in cluster.claims):
 450:                 out.append(cluster)
 451:         return tuple(out)
 452: 
 453:     def get_frame_coverage_for_entity(
 454:         self, entity_id: str
 455:     ) -> FrameCoverageEntry | None:
 456:         for entry in self.frame_coverage.entries:
 457:             if entry.entity_id == entity_id:
 458:                 return entry
 459:         return None
 460: 
 461:     def get_tier_counts(self) -> dict[str, int]:
 462:         return {
 463:             tier: int(round(frac * self.tier_mix.corpus_count))
 464:             for tier, frac in self.tier_mix.fractions.items()
 465:         }
 466: 
 467:     def get_sentence_by_claim_id(self, claim_id: str) -> ReportSentence | None:
 468:         """Foundation lookup for Evidence Inspector view 1 (Report click-to-inspect)."""
 469:         for section in self.verified_report.sections:
 470:             for sentence in section.sentences:
 471:                 if sentence.claim_id == claim_id:
 472:                     return sentence
 473:         return None
 474: 
 475:     def get_evidence_spans_for_claim(
 476:         self, claim_id: str
 477:     ) -> tuple[EvidenceSpanToken, ...]:
 478:         sentence = self.get_sentence_by_claim_id(claim_id)
 479:         return sentence.tokens if sentence is not None else ()

 482: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 483: # Loader internals
 484: # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 485: 
 486: 
 487: class AuditIRSchemaError(ValueError):
 488:     """Raised when an artifact directory violates the canonical schema."""
 489: 
 490: 
 491: def _read_json(path: Path) -> Any:
 492:     if not path.exists():
 493:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"Required artifact missing: {path}")
 494:     with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
 495:         return json.load(f)
 496: 
 497: 
 498: def _read_text(path: Path) -> str:
 499:     if not path.exists():
 500:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"Required artifact missing: {path}")
 501:     return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
 502: 
 503: 
 504: def _require_keys(d: Mapping[str, Any], keys: tuple[str, ...], where: str) -> None:
 505:     missing = [k for k in keys if k not in d]
 506:     if missing:
 507:         raise AuditIRSchemaError(
 508:             f"{where}: required keys missing: {missing}"
 509:         )
 510: 
 511: 
 512: def _parse_bibliography(raw: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> tuple[BibliographyEntry, ...]:
 513:     if not isinstance(raw, list):
 514:         raise AuditIRSchemaError("bibliography.json: expected a list")
 515:     out = []
 516:     for i, entry in enumerate(raw):
 517:         _require_keys(entry, ("num", "evidence_id"), f"bibliography[{i}]")
 518:         out.append(
 519:             BibliographyEntry(
 520:                 num=int(entry["num"]),
 521:                 evidence_id=str(entry["evidence_id"]),
 522:                 statement=str(entry.get("statement", "")),
 523:                 tier=str(entry.get("tier", "UNKNOWN")),
 524:                 url=str(entry.get("url", "")),
 525:             )
 526:         )
 527:     return tuple(out)
 528: 
 529: 
 530: def _parse_contradiction_claim(
 531:     raw: Mapping[str, Any], where: str
 532: ) -> ContradictionClaim:
 533:     _require_keys(raw, ("evidence_id", "predicate", "value"), where)
 534:     return ContradictionClaim(
 535:         evidence_id=str(raw["evidence_id"]),
 536:         subject=str(raw.get("subject", "")),
 537:         predicate=str(raw["predicate"]),
 538:         arm=str(raw.get("arm", "")),
 539:         dose=str(raw.get("dose", "")),
 540:         value=float(raw["value"]),
 541:         unit=str(raw.get("unit", "")),
 542:         source_tier=str(raw.get("source_tier", "UNKNOWN")),
 543:         source_url=str(raw.get("source_url", "")),
 544:         context_snippet=str(raw.get("context_snippet", "")),
 545:         endpoint_phrase=str(raw.get("endpoint_phrase", "")),
 546:     )
 547: 
 548: 
 549: def _parse_contradictions(
 550:     raw: list[dict[str, Any]],
 551: ) -> tuple[ContradictionCluster, ...]:
 552:     if not isinstance(raw, list):
 553:         raise AuditIRSchemaError("contradictions.json: expected a list")
 554:     clusters = []
 555:     for idx, raw_cluster in enumerate(raw):
 556:         where = f"contradictions[{idx}]"
 557:         _require_keys(raw_cluster, ("predicate", "claims"), where)
 558:         claims_raw = raw_cluster["claims"]
 559:         if not isinstance(claims_raw, list) or len(claims_raw) < 2:
 560:             raise AuditIRSchemaError(
 561:                 f"{where}: 'claims' must be a list of >=2 entries"
 562:             )
 563:         claims = tuple(
 564:             _parse_contradiction_claim(c, f"{where}.claims[{j}]")
 565:             for j, c in enumerate(claims_raw)
 566:         )
 567:         clusters.append(
 568:             ContradictionCluster(
 569:                 cluster_id=idx,
 570:                 subject=str(raw_cluster.get("subject", "")),
 571:                 predicate=str(raw_cluster["predicate"]),
 572:                 severity=str(raw_cluster.get("severity", "unknown")),
 573:                 absolute_difference=float(raw_cluster.get("absolute_difference", 0.0)),
 574:                 relative_difference=float(raw_cluster.get("relative_difference", 0.0)),
 575:                 recommended_action=str(raw_cluster.get("recommended_action", "")),
 576:                 claims=claims,
 577:             )
 578:         )
 579:     return tuple(clusters)
 580: 
 581: 
 582: def _parse_retrieval_attempt(raw: Mapping[str, Any]) -> RetrievalAttempt:
 583:     return RetrievalAttempt(
 584:         attempt_index=int(raw.get("attempt_index", 0)),
 585:         source=str(raw.get("source", "")),
 586:         url=str(raw.get("url", "")),
 587:         outcome=str(raw.get("outcome", "")),
 588:         http_status=(int(raw["http_status"]) if raw.get("http_status") is not None else None),
 589:     )
 590: 
 591: 
 592: def _parse_frame_coverage_entry(
 593:     raw: Mapping[str, Any], where: str
 594: ) -> FrameCoverageEntry:
 595:     _require_keys(raw, ("entity_id", "status"), where)
 596:     return FrameCoverageEntry(
 597:         entity_id=str(raw["entity_id"]),
 598:         entity_type=str(raw.get("entity_type", "")),
 599:         section=str(raw.get("section", "")),
 600:         slot_id=str(raw.get("slot_id", "")),
 601:         subsection_title=str(raw.get("subsection_title", "")),
 602:         status=str(raw["status"]),
 603:         doi=raw.get("doi"),
 604:         pmid=raw.get("pmid"),
 605:         failure_reason=raw.get("failure_reason"),
 606:         available_artifacts=tuple(raw.get("available_artifacts", [])),
 607:         required_fields=tuple(raw.get("required_fields", [])),

 succeeded in 1685ms:
   1: """Run-status response schema.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12): split lifecycle (operational) from pipeline_status
   4: (pipeline-A manifest verdict). Old `status` retained as computed alias for
   5: tests/v6/ backcompat — populated from lifecycle_status.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): `cancel_requested` surfaced so the UI can show a
   8: cancel as in-flight in <5s, before an in-progress run reaches the next
   9: pipeline stage boundary and transitions to terminal `cancelled`.
  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, computed_field
  17: 
  18: LifecycleStatus = Literal[
  19:     "queued",
  20:     "in_progress",
  21:     "completed",
  22:     "cancelled",
  23:     "failed",
  24: ]
  25: 
  26: PipelineStatus = Literal[
  27:     "success",
  28:     "partial_outline_fallback",
  29:     "partial_qwen_advisory",  # legacy alias (I-modref-004 #530) — historical manifests
  30:     "partial_evaluator_advisory",
  31:     "partial_thin_corpus",
  32:     "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  33:     "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  34:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  35:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  36:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  37:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  38:     "abort_no_sources",
  39:     "abort_evaluator_critical",
  40:     "error_unexpected",
  41: ]
  42: 
  43: # Backcompat alias used by older code/tests (tests/v6/ asserts body['status']
  44: # and record.status). Computed from lifecycle_status by the model.
  45: RunStatus = LifecycleStatus
  46: 
  47: 
  48: class RunStatusResponse(BaseModel):
  49:     run_id: str = Field(..., description="Server-assigned UUID hex.")
  50:     lifecycle_status: LifecycleStatus = Field(
  51:         ...,
  52:         description="Operational lifecycle: queued → in_progress → completed|failed|cancelled.",
  53:     )
  54:     pipeline_status: PipelineStatus | None = Field(
  55:         default=None,
  56:         description="Pipeline-A manifest verdict. NULL until run reaches a terminal pipeline state.",
  57:     )
  58:     template: str
  59:     question: str
  60:     queued_at: str = Field(..., description="ISO8601 UTC.")
  61:     started_at: str | None = None
  62:     finished_at: str | None = None
  63:     result_json: str | None = None
  64:     error_json: str | None = None
  65:     # I-arch-001a new optional fields for UUID/slug/artifact_dir mapping.
  66:     query_slug: str | None = None
  67:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None
  68:     artifact_dir: str | None = None
  69:     cost_usd: float | None = None
  70:     decision_id: str | None = None
  71:     # I-rdy-011: True once a cancel has been requested. For a queued run the
  72:     # request is applied atomically (lifecycle_status flips to 'cancelled');
  73:     # for an in_progress run this stays True while lifecycle_status is still
  74:     # 'in_progress', until the worker observes it at a stage boundary.
  75:     cancel_requested: bool = Field(
  76:         default=False,
  77:         description="True iff cancellation has been requested for this run.",
  78:     )
  79: 
  80:     @computed_field  # serialized in JSON and readable as attr
  81:     @property
  82:     def status(self) -> LifecycleStatus:

 842: def _parse_verified_report(raw: Mapping[str, Any]) -> VerifiedReport:
 843:     _require_keys(raw, ("sections", "totals"), "verification_details.json")
 844:     if not isinstance(raw["sections"], list):
 845:         raise AuditIRSchemaError("verification_details.json: 'sections' must be a list")
 846:     sections: list[ReportSection] = []
 847:     for sec in raw["sections"]:
 848:         title = str(sec.get("title", ""))
 849:         kept_raw = sec.get("kept", []) or []
 850:         dropped_raw = sec.get("dropped", []) or []
 851:         sentences = list(
 852:             _parse_verification_sentence(s, title, "kept", i)
 853:             for i, s in enumerate(kept_raw)
 854:         )
 855:         sentences.extend(
 856:             _parse_verification_sentence(s, title, "dropped", i)
 857:             for i, s in enumerate(dropped_raw)
 858:         )
 859:         sections.append(
 860:             ReportSection(
 861:                 title=title,
 862:                 kept_count=int(sec.get("total_kept", len(kept_raw))),
 863:                 dropped_count=int(sec.get("total_dropped", len(dropped_raw))),
 864:                 total_in=int(sec.get("total_in", 0)),
 865:                 dropped_due_to_failure=int(sec.get("dropped_due_to_failure", 0)),
 866:                 sentences=tuple(sentences),
 867:             )
 868:         )
 869:     totals = raw.get("totals", {}) or {}
 870:     drop_counts = raw.get("drop_reason_counts", {}) or {}
 871:     return VerifiedReport(
 872:         sections=tuple(sections),
 873:         sentences_verified=int(totals.get("sentences_verified", 0)),
 874:         sentences_dropped=int(totals.get("sentences_dropped", 0)),
 875:         drop_reason_counts=MappingProxyType(
 876:             {str(k): int(v) for k, v in drop_counts.items()}
 877:         ),
 878:     )

 890: def _parse_model_provenance(
 891:     eval_rules_raw: Mapping[str, Any] | None,
 892:     judge_raw: Mapping[str, Any] | None,
 893: ) -> ModelProvenance | None:
 894:     """Codex M-1 v2 review fix: load model/version provenance from runtime artifacts.
 895: 
 896:     Returns None if BOTH files are absent (legacy runs predate them).
 897:     Raises AuditIRSchemaError if exactly one is present, since partial
 898:     provenance silently zero-filling the missing half violates audit-grade
 899:     discipline (Codex M-1 v3 review edge case).
 900:     """
 901:     if eval_rules_raw is None and judge_raw is None:
 902:         return None
 903:     if eval_rules_raw is None or judge_raw is None:
 904:         present = "evaluator_rule_checks.json" if eval_rules_raw else "judge_output.json"
 905:         missing = "judge_output.json" if eval_rules_raw else "evaluator_rule_checks.json"
 906:         raise AuditIRSchemaError(
 907:             f"Partial model provenance: {present} present but {missing} missing. "
 908:             f"Both must be present together or both absent."
 909:         )
 910:     rule_checks = tuple(
 911:         _parse_rule_check(rc) for rc in eval_rules_raw.get("rule_checks", [])
 912:     )
 913:     return ModelProvenance(
 914:         generator_family=str(eval_rules_raw.get("generator_family", "")),
 915:         generator_model=str(eval_rules_raw.get("generator_model", "")),
 916:         evaluator_family=str(eval_rules_raw.get("evaluator_family", "")),
 917:         evaluator_model=str(eval_rules_raw.get("evaluator_model", "")),
 918:         judge_model=str(judge_raw.get("model", "")),
 919:         judge_parse_ok=bool(judge_raw.get("parse_ok", False)),
 920:         judge_input_tokens=int(judge_raw.get("input_tokens", 0)),
 921:         judge_output_tokens=int(judge_raw.get("output_tokens", 0)),
 922:         contradictions_disclosed=int(eval_rules_raw.get("contradictions_disclosed", 0)),
 923:         contradictions_missing=tuple(
 924:             str(c) for c in eval_rules_raw.get("contradictions_missing", [])
 925:         ),
 926:         rule_checks=rule_checks,
 927:     )

 969: def load_audit_ir(artifact_dir: Path | str) -> AuditIR:
 970:     """Load a V30 Phase-2 run artifact directory into a canonical AuditIR.
 971: 
 972:     Required files in artifact_dir:
 973:         manifest.json
 974:         report.md
 975:         bibliography.json
 976:         contradictions.json
 977:         verification_details.json
 978: 
 979:     Raises
 980:     ------
 981:     NotADirectoryError
 982:         If `artifact_dir` is not an existing directory.
 983:     FileNotFoundError
 984:         If any required file is missing.
 985:     AuditIRSchemaError
 986:         If any required schema block is missing or malformed. The IR fails
 987:         loud at load-time per audit-grade discipline; renderers should not
 988:         have to defensively fill in missing data.
 989:     """
 990:     artifact_dir = Path(artifact_dir)
 991:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
 992:         raise NotADirectoryError(f"artifact_dir is not a directory: {artifact_dir}")
 993: 
 994:     manifest_raw = _read_json(artifact_dir / "manifest.json")
 995:     if not isinstance(manifest_raw, Mapping):
 996:         raise AuditIRSchemaError("manifest.json: top-level must be a JSON object")
 997:     report_md = _read_text(artifact_dir / "report.md")
 998:     bibliography_raw = _read_json(artifact_dir / "bibliography.json")
 999:     contradictions_raw = _read_json(artifact_dir / "contradictions.json")
1000:     verification_raw = _read_json(artifact_dir / "verification_details.json")
1001: 
1002:     # Optional provenance files — present in V30 Phase-2 runs, absent in legacy.
1003:     eval_rules_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "evaluator_rule_checks.json")
1004:     judge_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "judge_output.json")
1005:     if judge_raw is None:
1006:         # I-modref-004 (#530): legacy artifact-name fallback — historical
1007:         # runs wrote qwen_judge_output.json; keep loading them.
1008:         judge_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "qwen_judge_output.json")
1009:     protocol_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "protocol.json")
1010:     corpus_approval_raw = _read_optional_json(artifact_dir / "corpus_approval.json")
1011: 
1012:     manifest = _parse_manifest(manifest_raw)
1013:     bibliography = _parse_bibliography(bibliography_raw)
1014:     contradictions = _parse_contradictions(contradictions_raw)
1015:     frame_coverage = _parse_frame_coverage(
1016:         manifest_raw.get("frame_coverage_report"),
1017:         manifest.v30_warnings,
1018:     )
1019:     tier_mix = _parse_tier_mix(manifest_raw.get("corpus"))
1020:     verified_report = _parse_verified_report(verification_raw)
1021:     model_provenance = _parse_model_provenance(eval_rules_raw, judge_raw)
1022:     protocol = _parse_protocol(protocol_raw)
1023:     adequacy = _parse_adequacy(manifest_raw.get("adequacy"))
1024:     corpus_approval = _parse_corpus_approval(corpus_approval_raw)
1025: 
1026:     return AuditIR(
1027:         ir_schema_version=IR_SCHEMA_VERSION,
1028:         run_id=manifest.run_id,
1029:         artifact_dir=artifact_dir,
1030:         report_md=report_md,
1031:         manifest=manifest,
1032:         bibliography=bibliography,
1033:         contradictions=contradictions,
1034:         frame_coverage=frame_coverage,
1035:         tier_mix=tier_mix,
1036:         verified_report=verified_report,
1037:         model_provenance=model_provenance,
1038:         protocol=protocol,
1039:         adequacy=adequacy,
1040:         corpus_approval=corpus_approval,

 100: def get_inspector_run(run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 101:     """Return the full faithful AuditIR for a completed run as a JSON dict.
 102: 
 103:     The canonical data source for the Evidence Inspector and every derivative
 104:     rich surface (I-rdy-008 #504, Option A). Resolution:
 105: 
 106:     - unknown run -> 404
 107:     - run not completed -> 409
 108:     - abort_* / error_* run -> 422 (no AuditIR-loadable artifacts)
 109:     - missing / absent artifact_dir -> 404
 110:     - artifact_dir present but unloadable -> 422 (fail loud, no zero-fill)
 111:     - completed loadable run -> 200, full AuditIR JSON
 112:     """
 113:     artifact_dir = resolve_completed_artifact_dir(run_id)
 114: 
 115:     try:
 116:         ir = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 117:     except (FileNotFoundError, NotADirectoryError, ValueError, TypeError) as exc:
 118:         # AuditIRSchemaError and json.JSONDecodeError are both ValueError
 119:         # subclasses; plain ValueError / TypeError also catch malformed
 120:         # numeric fields (Codex brief iter-2 P2). Fail loud per audit-grade
 121:         # discipline — no silent zero-fill of canonical structures.
 122:         raise HTTPException(
 123:             status_code=422,
 124:             detail=f"run {run_id} artifact_dir failed AuditIR load: {exc}",
 125:         ) from exc
 126: 
 127:     return to_json_dict(ir)

 131: def get_inspector_run_evidence(run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
 132:     """Return the verified evidence spans cited by a completed run.
 133: 
 134:     I-rdy-008 (#504) slice 7a (Codex arch consult
 135:     `.codex/I-rdy-008/slice7_arch_consult_verdict.txt`). Every verified-report
 136:     sentence carries `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` tokens; this route resolves
 137:     each token's `evidence_id` against `evidence_pool.json` and reconstructs
 138:     the exact cited span as `body[start:end]` — the auditable source text an
 139:     auditor verifies a claim against. Spans are range-keyed
 140:     (`evidence_id, start, end`) and de-duplicated; `claim_ids` lists every
 141:     sentence that cites the span.
 142: 
 143:     Fails loud (422) — never degrades to a bibliography statement — when
 144:     `evidence_pool.json` is absent/malformed, a token cites an evidence id
 145:     absent from the pool, a row has no body text, or a token's offsets are
 146:     out of range.
 147: 
 148:     Resolution: unknown 404 / not-completed 409 / abort 422 / missing
 149:     artifact_dir 404 / unloadable AuditIR 422 / no evidence_pool.json 422 /
 150:     completed + loadable + pooled -> 200.
 151:     """
 152:     artifact_dir = resolve_completed_artifact_dir(run_id)
 153:     pool = _load_evidence_pool(artifact_dir, run_id)
 154: 
 155:     try:
 156:         ir = load_audit_ir(artifact_dir)
 157:     except (FileNotFoundError, NotADirectoryError, ValueError, TypeError) as exc:
 158:         raise HTTPException(
 159:             status_code=422,
 160:             detail=f"run {run_id} artifact_dir failed AuditIR load: {exc}",
 161:         ) from exc
 162: 
 163:     # Range key (evidence_id, start, end) -> set of citing sentence claim_ids.

 166:         for sentence in section.sentences:
 167:             for token in sentence.tokens:

   1: """Shared completed-run resolver for the v6 rich-surface read routes.
   2: 
   3: I-rdy-008 (#504) slice 8: `resolve_completed_artifact_dir` was first added
   4: in slice 7a inside `inspector.py` (as `_resolve_completed_artifact_dir`).
   5: The charts route (slice 8) needs the identical `run_store -> artifact_dir`
   6: resolution, so it is extracted here as the single shared implementation —
   7: behavior is unchanged: same status codes, same detail strings.
   8: """
   9: 
  10: from __future__ import annotations
  11: 
  12: from pathlib import Path
  13: 
  14: from fastapi import HTTPException
  15: 
  16: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  17: 
  18: 
  19: def resolve_completed_artifact_dir(run_id: str) -> Path:
  20:     """Resolve a completed run to its on-disk artifact_dir, or raise.
  21: 
  22:     The shared run-resolution for every completed-run read route (inspector
  23:     slices 1 + 7a, charts slice 8):
  24: 
  25:     - unknown run -> 404
  26:     - run not completed -> 409
  27:     - abort_* / error_* run -> 422 (no AuditIR-loadable artifacts)
  28:     - missing / absent artifact_dir -> 404
  29:     """
  30:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  31:     if record is None:
  32:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run not found: {run_id}")
  33: 
  34:     if record.lifecycle_status != "completed":
  35:         raise HTTPException(
  36:             status_code=409,
  37:             detail=(
  38:                 f"run {run_id} is not completed "
  39:                 f"(lifecycle_status={record.lifecycle_status!r})"
  40:             ),
  41:         )
  42: 
  43:     status = record.pipeline_status or ""
  44:     if status.startswith("abort_") or status.startswith("error_"):
  45:         raise HTTPException(
  46:             status_code=422,
  47:             detail=(
  48:                 f"run {run_id} produced no AuditIR-loadable artifacts "
  49:                 f"(pipeline_status={status!r}); it is a pipeline-verdict "
  50:                 f"artifact, not a renderable run"
  51:             ),
  52:         )
  53: 
  54:     if not record.artifact_dir:
  55:         raise HTTPException(
  56:             status_code=404,
  57:             detail=f"run {run_id} has no artifact_dir recorded",
  58:         )
  59:     artifact_dir = Path(record.artifact_dir)
  60:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
  61:         raise HTTPException(
  62:             status_code=404,
  63:             detail=f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}",
  64:         )
  65:     return artifact_dir

with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory(dir='C:/tmp') as td:

    manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text())
    manifest['status'] = 'partial_evaluator_advisory'
    manifest['release_allowed'] = False
    manifest['evaluator_gate']['release_allowed'] = False
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(manifest, sort_keys=True))

    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(db))
    conn.execute(
        \"INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at, started_at, finished_at, artifact_dir, pipeline_status, cancel_requested) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,0)\",

    )

# Codex DECISION consult — I-cd-680 scope (PHASE 1)

Operator delegates scope decisions to Codex, highest long-term quality. Decide the scope of #680.

## The fork

#680 as written = a 600-1000 LOC pipeline-A capability extension: thread per-sentence provenance + per-evidence-span char-offsets (span_start/span_end) through run_one_query + the verifier, emit a typed EvidenceContract JSON. Its OWN sequencing note says: "Defer to AFTER the demo. Inspector currently consumes the slice-chain bundle.tar.gz path which is sufficient for Carney delivery. EvidenceContract is a Phase-2 capability."

BUT the 2026-05-20 re-prioritization (your APPROVE) put #680 in PHASE 1 as the foundation that unblocks #542 (follow-up UI) + #543 (compare view), which you flagged as fixture-only (404 on real runs).

## Verified facts (grep, this branch)

- `src/polaris_v6/api/followup.py:24` + `compare.py:18` resolve run_id ONLY via `_GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX` (golden fixtures) → real runs 404. THIS is the #542/#543 blocker.
- `src/polaris_v6/api/bundle.py:89` `GET /runs/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz` ALREADY resolves real run_id → artifact_dir → signed bundle via run_store (I-cd-020 Option D). Inspector (#631) consumes this and works on real runs.
- So the inspector real-run path EXISTS; only followup + compare are fixture-locked.

## The question

For PHASE 1 (unblock #542/#543 for the demo), is the right scope:

A. **Full #680** — build the 600-1000 LOC EvidenceContract char-offset capability now. (Issue says defer post-demo; LAW II fabrication risk on synthesizing offsets pipeline-A never recorded.)

B. **Minimal real-run resolution** — make followup.py + compare.py resolve real run_id → artifact_dir → the EXISTING slice-chain data (same path bundle.tar.gz uses), so #542/#543 work on real completed runs WITHOUT the full char-offset EvidenceContract. Defer the full EvidenceContract capability (char offsets + per-sentence JSON) to a post-demo Phase-2 issue.

C. Something else.

My engineering read: B. The demo needs followup + compare to WORK on real runs (the operator's PHASE-2 UI goal), not the full Phase-2 EvidenceContract JSON. The full capability is genuinely post-demo per the issue's own note + carries fabrication risk. B unblocks #542/#543 with the data that already exists; A builds 1000 LOC the demo doesn't need + risks LAW II.

Decide A/B/C. If B, confirm the deferred full-capability becomes a new post-demo issue. Highest long-term quality lens.

codex
Decision: **B**.

For Phase 1, scope #680 to **minimal real-run resolution for followup + compare**:

- Resolve `run_id -> artifact_dir` through the same `run_store` path already proven by `GET /runs/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz`.
- Load the existing slice-chain data that Inspector already consumes.
- Preserve golden fixture support where needed.
- Do **not** synthesize `span_start` / `span_end`.
- Do **not** introduce the full typed `EvidenceContract` JSON in Phase 1.

This is the higher-quality choice because the actual blocker for #542/#543 is not missing char-offset provenance; it is that `followup.py` and `compare.py` are fixture-locked via `_GOLDEN_RUN_INDEX`. Building full EvidenceContract now would expand scope, increase regression risk, and create LAW II risk if offsets are inferred rather than recorded by Pipeline A.

I would frame the Phase 1 acceptance criteria as:

1. Real completed runs no longer 404 in follow-up and compare.
2. Both APIs resolve real `run_id` using `run_store`.
3. They consume existing artifact/slice-chain data only.
4. Golden fixture behavior remains intact.
5. Tests cover real-run resolution and missing-artifact failure modes.
6. No fabricated char offsets are emitted.

Yes: the full capability should become a **new post-demo Phase 2 issue** or be explicitly split out from #680. That issue should cover the real EvidenceContract design: Pipeline A records offsets at source, verifier threads them through, and APIs emit typed evidence spans only when grounded offsets exist.
